  <script type="text/javascript">
   //Email Capture For Quote

    var emailCapture = Class.create();
    emailCapture.prototype = {
        initialize: function(options) {
            this.options = Object.extend({
                elements: "input[name='billing[email]']"
            }, options || {} );

            // Observe blur on email field
            $$(this.options.elements).each(function(email) {
                Event.observe(email,'blur',this.captureEmail.bindAsEventListener(this));
            }.bind(this));
        },

        //capture email
        captureEmail: function(event) {
            var el = $(Event.element(event));
            //validate email
            if(el.value && this.validateEmail(el.value)){
                //ajax call
                new Ajax.Request('https://hobbyking.com/de_de/' + 'connector/ajax/emailcapture', {
                    method: 'post',
                    parameters:{
                        email:el.value
                    }
                });
            }
        },

        //email validation
        validateEmail: function (email) {
            var re = /^(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
            return re.test(email);
        }
    };

    //Email Capture For Newsletter

    var newsletterEmailCapture = Class.create();
    newsletterEmailCapture.prototype = {
        initialize: function(options) {
            this.options = Object.extend({
                elements: "input[name='email']"
            }, options || {} );

            // Observe blur on email field
            $$(this.options.elements).each(function(email) {
                Event.observe(email,'blur',this.captureEmail.bindAsEventListener(this));
            }.bind(this));
        },

        //capture email
        captureEmail: function(event) {
            var el = $(Event.element(event));
            //validate email
            if(el.value && this.validateEmail(el.value)){
                //ajax call
                new Ajax.Request('https://hobbyking.com/de_de/' + 'connector/ajax/emailcapture', {
                    method: 'post',
                    parameters:{
                        email:el.value
                    }
                });
            }
        },

        //email validation
        validateEmail: function (email) {
            var re = /^(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
            return re.test(email);
        }
    };
  </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     jQuery(document).ready(function () {
        function init() {
            jQuery('#mobileFloatProceedCheckout').css({
                'display': 'none'
            });
        }

        function showMobileProceedCheckoutBtn() {
            jQuery('#mobileFloatProceedCheckout').css({
                'display': 'block'
            });
        }

        function hideMobileProceedCheckoutBtn() {
            jQuery('#mobileFloatProceedCheckout').css({
                'display': 'none'
            });
        }

        jQuery('body').click(function (evt) {
            if (evt.target.id == "mobileFloatProceedCheckout")
                return;
            if (evt.target.id == "cartadd")
                return;
            if (jQuery(evt.target).closest('#mobileFloatProceedCheckout').length)
                return;
            if (jQuery(evt.target).closest('#cartadd').length)
                return;
            jQuery('#mobileFloatProceedCheckout').css({
                'display': 'none'
            });
        });

        init();
        var $mobileWidth = jQuery(window).width();
        if ($mobileWidth  <=  1024 ) {
            jQuery('.wrp-floating-cart > .place-floating-cart > .floating-checkout-btn').click(function () {
                showMobileProceedCheckoutBtn();
            });
        }
    });
//Jquery script for the shake animation when user click the add to cart button.	
$j(function(){
$j('.-js-btn-ajax').click(function(){
        function shakeFloatCartContFunc() {
            var floatCartCont = $j('#floating-cart .place-floating-cart a.floating-checkout-btn');
            floatCartCont.animate({
                right: '25px'
            }, 100);
            floatCartCont.animate({
                right: '20px'
            }, 100);
            floatCartCont.animate({
                right: '25px'
            }, 100);
            floatCartCont.animate({
                right: '20px'
            }, 100);
            floatCartCont.animate({
                right: '25px'
            }, 100);
            floatCartCont.animate({
                right: '20px'
            }, 100);   
        }
        function shakeFloatCartLoaderFunc() {
            var floatCartLoader = $j('#floating-cart .place-floating-cart img.floating-loader-image');
            floatCartLoader.animate({
                right: '37px'
            }, 100);
            floatCartLoader.animate({
                right: '32px'
            }, 100);
            floatCartLoader.animate({
                right: '37px'
            }, 100);
            floatCartLoader.animate({
                right: '32px'
            }, 100);
            floatCartLoader.animate({
                right: '37px'
            }, 100);
            floatCartLoader.animate({
                right: '32px'
            }, 100);
        }
        shakeFloatCartContFunc();
        shakeFloatCartLoaderFunc();
    });
});
    </script>

         jQuery(function() {

                    items: 4
                },
                640: {
                    items: 6
                },
                768: {
                    items: 6
                },
                800: {
                    items: 6
                },
                900: {
                    items: 6
                },
                960: {
                    items: 6
                },
                999: {
                    items: 6
                }
            }
        });

        // remove the product category names from tablet to mobile views after certain scrolling
        var mobCarouselProdCatWindowWidth = jQuery(window).width();

        if (mobCarouselProdCatWindowWidth <= 999) {
            jQuery(window).scroll(function () {
                var mobCarouselProdCatScrollTopVal = jQuery(this).scrollTop();
                var mobCarouselProdCatName = jQuery('#mobile-prod-cat-owl .mobile-prod-cat-carousel .item a span.contents h2.product-category-name');
                var mobCarouselProdCatCont = jQuery('#mobile-prod-cat-owl .mobile-prod-cat-carousel .item a span.contents');
                var mobProdCatOwl = jQuery('#mobile-prod-cat-owl');

                if (mobCarouselProdCatScrollTopVal >= 200) {
                    mobProdCatOwl.addClass('hide');
                    mobProdCatOwl.css({
                        'top': '50px'
                    });
                    jQuery('.wrapper .page .main-container .main .col-main .slider-wrapper').css({
                        'margin-top': '116px'
                    });
                    jQuery('.wrapper .page .sticky-header-banner-carousel-bar').css({
                        'display': 'none'
                    });
                    jQuery('.wrapper .page .header-top').css({
                        'margin-top': '0px'
                    });
                }
                else {
                    mobProdCatOwl.removeClass('hide');
                    jQuery('.wrapper .page .sticky-header-banner-carousel-bar').css({
                        'display': 'block'
                    });
                }
            });
        }
    })
        </script>

              <script type="text/javascript">
               document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
        var hotCarousel = {
            carousel: $j('#hot-carousel'),
            breakpoint: {
                sm: 480,
                md: 1000
            },
            owlConfig: {
                navText: ['<i class="fa fa-angle-left" aria-hidden="true"></i>',
                    '<i class="fa fa-angle-right" aria-hidden="true"></i>'],
                nav: true,
                dots: false,
                loop: true,
                margin: 20,
                rewind: true,
                lazyLoad: true,
                responsive: {
                    0: {
                        items: 1,
                        slideBy: 1,
                        margin: 0
                    },
                    480: {
                        items: 2,
                        slideBy: 1
                    },
                    1000: {
                        items: 3,
                        slideBy: 1
                    },
                    1300: {
                        items: 4,
                        slideBy: 1
                    }
                },
                onInitialized: function () {
                    carouselInit.checkInitializedAllCarouselItem();
                    
                    $$('.cloned .wishlist-selector').each(function(one){
                       Event.observe(one.down('.change'), 'click', function(event){
                           Event.stop(event);
                           if (one.hasClassName('active')) {
                               one.removeClassName.bind(one, 'active').delay(0.2);
                           } else {
                               one.addClassName.bind(one, 'active').delay(0.2);
                           }
                       });
                        Event.observe(one.down('.change'), 'blur', function(event){
                            Event.stop(event);
                            one.removeClassName.bind(one, 'active').delay(0.2);
                        });

                          one.select('ul li').each(function(li){
                                Event.observe(li, 'click', function(event){
                                    if(li.getAttribute('data-url') && !li.classList.contains('new')){
                                        window.location.href = li.getAttribute('data-url');
                                    }
                                    else if(li.classList.contains('new')){
                                        Enterprise.Wishlist.createWithCallback(Enterprise.Wishlist.url.create, function(wishlistId) {
                                            console.log(arguments);
                                            var _listName = document.getElementById('wishlist-name');
                                            if(_listName && _listName.value){
                                                window.location.href = li.getAttribute('data-url')+'?wishlist_id='+wishlistId;
                                            }
                                        }, true);
                                    }

                                });
                          });
                    });
                }
            }
        }

        carouselInit.initialize(hotCarousel);
    });
              </script>

            <script type="text/javascript">
             document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
        var hotCarousel = {
            carousel: $j('#hot-carousel'),
            breakpoint: {
                sm: 480,
                md: 1000
            },
            owlConfig: {
                navText: ['<i class="fa fa-angle-left" aria-hidden="true"></i>',
                    '<i class="fa fa-angle-right" aria-hidden="true"></i>'],
                nav: true,
                dots: false,
                loop: true,
                margin: 20,
                rewind: true,
                lazyLoad: true,
                responsive: {
                    0: {
                        items: 1,
                        slideBy: 1,
                        margin: 0
                    },
                    480: {
                        items: 2,
                        slideBy: 1
                    },
                    1000: {
                        items: 3,
                        slideBy: 1
                    },
                    1300: {
                        items: 4,
                        slideBy: 1
                    }
                },
                onInitialized: function () {
                    carouselInit.checkInitializedAllCarouselItem();
                    
                    $$('.cloned .wishlist-selector').each(function(one){
                       Event.observe(one.down('.change'), 'click', function(event){
                           Event.stop(event);
                           if (one.hasClassName('active')) {
                               one.removeClassName.bind(one, 'active').delay(0.2);
                           } else {
                               one.addClassName.bind(one, 'active').delay(0.2);
                           }
                       });
                        Event.observe(one.down('.change'), 'blur', function(event){
                            Event.stop(event);
                            one.removeClassName.bind(one, 'active').delay(0.2);
                        });

                          one.select('ul li').each(function(li){
                                Event.observe(li, 'click', function(event){
                                    if(li.getAttribute('data-url') && !li.classList.contains('new')){
                                        window.location.href = li.getAttribute('data-url');
                                    }
                                    else if(li.classList.contains('new')){
                                        Enterprise.Wishlist.createWithCallback(Enterprise.Wishlist.url.create, function(wishlistId) {
                                            console.log(arguments);
                                            var _listName = document.getElementById('wishlist-name');
                                            if(_listName && _listName.value){
                                                window.location.href = li.getAttribute('data-url')+'?wishlist_id='+wishlistId;
                                            }
                                        }, true);
                                    }

                                });
                          });
                    });
                }
            }
        }

        carouselInit.initialize(hotCarousel);
    });

                      jQuery(this).find('img').removeAttr('style');
                  })
                  jQuery('.lazy-img-desk').lazy({
                      removeAttribute: false
                  });
              }

    <script type="text/javascript">
     function acceptCookieAlert() {
    Mage.Cookies.set('cookieAlertState', 1, new Date(new Date().getTime() + (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 364)));
    document.getElementById('cookiealert').style.display = 'none';
}

function declineCookieAlert() {
    closeCookieAlert();
    Mage.Cookies.set('cookieAlertState', 0, new Date(new Date().getTime() + (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 364)));
}

function loadCookieScript() {
}

if (!Mage.Cookies.get('cookieAlertState')) {
    document.getElementById('cookiealert').style.display = '';
}
    </script>
